# Competitive Programming
This repository contains my solutions to various competitive programming problems, 
which notably includes over 1.7k Kattis problems.

## Kattis Statistics
Last updated: 2025-10-19

* Problems solved: 1725
* Score: 4522.4
* Global rank: #70
* Norway rank: #3
